Models effective conflict resolution skills and effectively resolves any conflicts in a timely and respectful manner to achieve positive and healthy working relationships and workplace environment.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Promotes a quality-first work ethic and attitude to provide a product that is manufactured of the highest standard achievable.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Maintains confidentiality to comply with all regulatory requirements and Company Privacy and Confidentiality policies and procedures.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Understands, complies with, and is accountable for adherence to COR quality standards in all activities.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Safely operates company owned, leased, managed, or rented vehicles and\u002For mobile equipment. Performs and directly manages working level positions who perform Safety Sensitive duties and responsibilities.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Manages assigned tasks\u002Fprojects within scope of responsibility so all KPIs are achieved, including but not limited to safety, productivity, and product quality.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Establishs and manages the day-to-day priorities of the process and the crew.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Effectively manages the shift crew’s productivity including but not limited to having each crew member at their designated stations. Properly directs employees during interruptions in production by assigning alternative tasks to add value to the MRF.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Maintains efficient work flow by monitoring steps of the process, checking and verifying process variable settings and issues, observing equipment, monitoring staff and resources, and initiating and fostering a spirit of cooperation within and between shifts and departments.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Documents and communicates daily production activities to other MRF leadership team members.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Operates process related equipment including conveyors and hydraulic equipment as required. May also operate additional plant equipment such as loaders, grapple, forklifts, and other rolling stock. Provides coverage for a variety of stages in the process during periods of staff shortages or during special project work.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Troubleshoots technical and mechanical problems with plant equipment and investigates production and quality issues on a day to day basis.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Requests maintenance and repairs as required to facilitate continuous operation.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Manages and performs clean-up duties as assigned.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Writes and updates standard operating procedures for operation of production equipment as required.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Participates in the development of strategies to improve productivity, lower downtime, and operating cost adding value to the MRF. plant Production Standard Operating Procedures (SOPs).<\u002Fli>\n <li>Actively supports other initiatives of the Plant to promote a healthy and positive work environment and enhance employee morale and engagement.<\u002Fli>\n <li>Completes other duties as assigned.<\u002Fli>\n<\u002Ful>\n<p><b>Qualifications<\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n<ul>\n <li>Formal Education Required: High School Diploma or <\u002Fb><\u002Fp>\n<ul>\n <li>Accomplir divers travaux reliés à la vérification, réparation, entretien et nettoyage des systèmes de plomberie;<\u002Fli>\n <li>Assembler, réparer, mettre en place et entretient les canalisations d'air, de gaz, d'eau, de vapeur, d'égout et de plomberie sanitaire;<\u002Fli>\n <li>Assure le suivi des demandes de service et contrôle les interventions réalisées;<\u002Fli>\n<\u002Ful>\n<p>Effectuer les travaux d’urgence et de dépannage en entretien, réparation et modification des systèmes de plomberie;<\u002Fp>\n<ul>\n <li>Effectuer les travaux d’entretien préventif et correctif à l’aide du système de gestion de l’entretien GMAO, participer à la mise en place du plan et des gammes de maintenance des systèmes de plomberie;<\u002Fli>\n les urinoirs, les cabinets et les évents;<\u002Fp>\n<ul>\n <li>Chercher et régler les causes des problèmes;<\u002Fli>\n <li>Lire des plans, dessin et devis afin de de déterminer la disposition de la tuyauterie des réseaux d’alimentation;<\u002Fli>\n <li>Effectuer toutes autres tâches connexes.<\u002Fli>\n<\u002Ful>\n<p><b>Qualifications<\u002Fb><br><b>Exigences requises:
